r.attr("data-name")&&(i.name=r.attr("data-name")),0<r.parents(".ps-online-seller-select[data-name]").length&&(i.name=r.parents(".ps-online-seller-select[data-name]:first").attr("data-name")),r.attr("data-bi-prtnm")&&(i.retailer=r.attr("data-bi-prtnm")),null!=i.retailer&&""!=i.retailer||!r.attr("data-retailer")||(i.retailer=r.attr("data-retailer")||""),(null==i.retailer||""==i.retailer)&&0<r.parents("[data-retailer]").length&&(i.retailer=r.parents("[data-retailer]:first").attr("data-retailer")),i}}),!0)}),window.utf_event&&window.utf_event.trigger("frameworkLoaded"),window.utfLoaded=!0;
</script></body></html>
